--area

CREATE TABLE AREA 
(
  AREA_IDX NUMBER NOT NULL 
, NAME VARCHAR2(20 BYTE) 
, LATITUDE NUMBER 
, LONGTITUDE NUMBER 
, CONSTRAINT AREA_PK PRIMARY KEY 
  (
    AREA_IDX 
  )
  USING INDEX 
  (
      CREATE UNIQUE INDEX AREA_PK ON AREA (AREA_IDX ASC) 
      LOGGING 
      TABLESPACE SYSTEM 
      PCTFREE 10 
      INITRANS 2 
      STORAGE 
      ( 
        INITIAL 65536 
        NEXT 1048576 
        MINEXTENTS 1 
        MAXEXTENTS UNLIMITED 
        FREELISTS 1 
        FREELIST GROUPS 1 
        BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT 
      ) 
      NOPARALLEL 
  )
  ENABLE 
) 
LOGGING 
TABLESPACE SYSTEM 
PCTFREE 10 
PCTUSED 40 
INITRANS 1 
STORAGE 
( 
  INITIAL 65536 
  NEXT 1048576 
  MINEXTENTS 1 
  MAXEXTENTS UNLIMITED 
  FREELISTS 1 
  FREELIST GROUPS 1 
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT 
) 
NOPARALLEL;

COMMENT ON COLUMN AREA.AREA_IDX IS '지역 idx';

COMMENT ON COLUMN AREA.NAME IS '지역명';

COMMENT ON COLUMN AREA.LATITUDE IS '위도';

COMMENT ON COLUMN AREA.LONGTITUDE IS '경도';

CREATE TABLE MESSAGE 
(
  MESSAGE_IDX NUMBER NOT NULL 
, CHAT_IDX NUMBER 
, MEMBER_IDX NUMBER 
, CONTENT VARCHAR2(4000 BYTE) 
, SEND_DATE DATE 
, CONSTRAINT MESSAGE_PK PRIMARY KEY 
  (
    MESSAGE_IDX 
  )
  USING INDEX 
  (
      CREATE UNIQUE INDEX MESSAGE_PK ON MESSAGE (MESSAGE_IDX ASC)

      STORAGE

        BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT 
      ) 
      NOPARALLEL 
  )
  ENABLE 
)
